namespace = POP_Estates_Interactions

### By Demian

country_event = { ### Assess Greater Nobles Power
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.001
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.001.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.001.d"
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = eastern } picture = EE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = chinese } picture = EA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_GN_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_infantry	value = 1 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_infantry	value = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_cavalry	value = 1 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_cavalry	value = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_artillery	value = 1 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_artillery	value = 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { which = privilege_level 	value = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = commoners_banned_from_officers_corps_1_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = commoners_banned_from_officers_corps_2_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ceremonial_generalships_1_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ceremonial_generalships_2_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_relaxed_levy_obligations_1_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_relaxed_levy_obligations_2_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_tax_exemptions_1_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_tax_exemptions_2_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_tax_exemptions_3_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 3 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_tax_exemptions_4_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 4 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_exclude_commoners_cabinet_1_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_exclude_commoners_cabinet_2_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_high_court_titles_1_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_high_court_titles_2_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_high_nobles_court_1_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_high_nobles_court_2_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_authority_to_govern_locally_1_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_authority_to_govern_locally_2_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_authority_to_govern_locally_3_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 3 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GN_authority_to_govern_locally_4_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 4 }
			}
			
			#set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_power 		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_power 		which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_power 	value = 100 }
		}
	}
	
	# Assess Privileges
	option = {
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.001.a"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Interactions.0012 }
		}
	}
	
	# Levy details
	option = {
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.001.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = POP_Estates_Interactions.0011
			}
		}
	}
	
	#option = {
	#	name = back
	#	highlight = yes
	#	
	#	trigger = {
	#		ai = no
	#		NOT = { has_dlc = "The Cossacks" }
	#	}
	#	
	#	country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Menu.020 }
	#}
	
	option = {
		name = exit
		highlight = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_power 		value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = privilege_level 	value = 0 }
	}
}

country_event = { ### Assess Greater Nobles Power
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.0011
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.0011.t"
	desc = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_army_maintenance value = 0.001 } }
		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.0011.da"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_army_maintenance value = 0.001 } } }
		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.0011.db"
	}
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = eastern } picture = EE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = chinese } picture = EA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_GN_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_infantry	value = 1 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_infantry	value = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_cavalry	value = 1 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_cavalry	value = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_artillery	value = 1 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_artillery	value = 0 }
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_infantry_forcelimit	value = 1 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_infantry_forcelimit	value = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_cavalry_forcelimit	value = 1 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_cavalry_forcelimit	value = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_artillery_forcelimit	value = 1 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_artillery_forcelimit	value = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = back
		highlight = yes
		
		trigger = {
			ai = no
		}
		
		country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Interactions.001 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = exit
		highlight = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = { ### Offer Privileges Greater Nobles
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.002
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.002.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.002.d"
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = eastern } picture = EE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = chinese } picture = EA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_GN_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = PrivilegeGrantingOngoing
			#set_variable = { which = estate_weight_share 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = estate_weight_share 				which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
			set_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a 	value = 20 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a			value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a			value = 1000 }
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				#set_variable = { 	  which = GN_corruption_current 		value = 0 }
				set_variable = {   which = GN_corruption_current 		which = privilege_corruption_GN }
				multiply_variable = {   which = GN_corruption_current			value = 0.01 }
				
				set_variable = {      which = GN_corruption_cost_1 			value = 0.1 }
				multiply_variable = { which = GN_corruption_cost_1			which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
				
				#	set_variable = {      which = GN_corruption_cost_2 			value = 0 }
				#	change_variable = {   which = GN_corruption_cost_2 			value = 10 }
				#	multiply_variable = { which = GN_corruption_cost_2 			value = 2 }
				#	multiply_variable = {   which = GN_corruption_cost_2			value = 0.01 }
				#	multiply_variable = { which = GN_corruption_cost_2			which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
			}
			#set_variable = { 	  which = privilege_stability_gain 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = privilege_stability_gain 				which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
			#	change_variable = {   which = privilege_stability_gain				value = 0.15 }
			multiply_variable = { which = privilege_stability_gain 				value = 100 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = privilege_ticker_greater_nobles value = 40 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = temp value = 40 }
				subtract_variable = { which = temp which = privilege_ticker_greater_nobles }
				multiply_variable = { which = temp value = 0.025 }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { which = temp value = 0 }
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a which = temp }
			multiply_variable = { which = privilege_stability_gain which = temp }
			check_stability_modifier = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Ban Commoners From officer corps Rank 1
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.002.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = commoners_banned_from_officers_corps_1_flag }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = commoners_banned_from_officers_corps_2_flag }
		}
		commoners_banned_from_officers_corps_1 = yes
		custom_tooltip = estate_greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a
		custom_tooltip = privilege_stability_gain
		GN_corruption_added_1_tooltip_effect = yes
		custom_tooltip = commoners_banned_from_officers_corps_1_privilege_desc
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added		which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a }
			estate_greater_nobles_loyalty_added = yes
			change_variable = { which = stability_points 				which = privilege_stability_gain }
			set_variable = {    which = privilege_stability_gain 		value = 0  }
			set_variable = {    which = estate_weight_share 			value = 0  }
			set_variable = { which = GN_privileges_time_left            value = 60 }
			subtract_variable = { which = privilege_demand_ticker_greater_nobles		value = 40 }
			check_stability_gain = yes
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_global_flag = show_for_developers
			#	}
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_GN_privileges_bestowed 		value = 1 }
			#}
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Commoners Banned From Officers Corps Rank 2
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.002.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = commoners_banned_from_officers_corps_1_flag
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = commoners_banned_from_officers_corps_2_flag
			}
		}
		remove_commoners_banned_from_officers_corps_1 = yes
		commoners_banned_from_officers_corps_2 = yes
		custom_tooltip = estate_greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a
		custom_tooltip = privilege_stability_gain

country_event = { ### Offer Favors
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.003
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.003.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.003.d"
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = eastern } picture = EE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = chinese } picture = EA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_GN_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a 		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a 		value = 5 }
			#set_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_b 		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_b 		value = 5 }
			check_stability_modifier = yes
			set_variable = {	  which = diplo_cost_a 							value = 30 } ### Diplomatic cost for Honoring
			multiply_variable = { which = diplo_cost_a 							which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = {   which = diplo_cost_a 							value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = diplo_cost_a 							value = 1000 }
			set_variable = {	  which = diplo_cost_b 							value = 90 } ### Diplomatic cost for gift
			multiply_variable = { which = diplo_cost_b 							which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = {   which = diplo_cost_b							value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = diplo_cost_b 							value = 1000 }
			
			#set_variable = { which = prestige_available 	value = 0 }
			export_to_variable = {
				which = prestige_available
				value = prestige
			}
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = greater_nobles_prestige_demand 	value = 0 }
			set_variable = {	  which = greater_nobles_prestige_demand 	which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = greater_nobles_prestige_demand	value = 60 }
			set_variable = { which = prestige_needed 						which = greater_nobles_prestige_demand }
			divide_variable = {   which = prestige_needed					value = 10000 }
			multiply_variable = { which = prestige_needed					value = 10000 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = prestige_needed				value = 50 }
				}
				set_variable = { which = prestige_needed					value = 50 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = prestige_needed		value = 10 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = prestige_needed					value = 1 }
			}
			# set_variable = { 	  which = greater_nobles_prestige_trigger 	value = 0 }
			# set_variable = { 	  which = greater_nobles_prestige_trigger	which = prestige_available }
			# subtract_variable = { which = greater_nobles_prestige_trigger	which = greater_nobles_prestige_demand }
			#set_variable = { 	  which = prestige_stability_gain 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = prestige_stability_gain			which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = prestige_stability_gain 			value = 20 }

			#set_variable = { 	  which = ducat_cost_a 					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = ducat_cost_a 					which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_country }
			divide_variable = {   which = ducat_cost_a					value = 1.5 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = ducat_cost_a				value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = ducat_cost_a					value = 1000 }
			#set_variable = { 	  which = gift_stability_gain 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = gift_stability_gain			which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = gift_stability_gain 			value = 30 }

			#set_variable = { 	  which = corruption_cost 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = corruption_cost 				which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = corruption_cost				value = 10 }
			#set_variable = { 	  which = corruption_stability_gain 	value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = corruption_stability_gain		which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = corruption_stability_gain 	value = 20 }
			
			export_to_variable = { which = tmpTreasury value = treasury }
		}
	}
	
	# Honour a Noble House
	option = {
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.003.a"

			factor = 10000
		}

			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = greater_nobles_prestige_demand 			value = 10 }

			#	limit = {
			#		has_global_flag = show_for_developers
			#	}
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_GN_favors_offered 							value = 1 }
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_GN_cabinet_posts 							value = 1 }
			#}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 0 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 1 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 1 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 2 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 2 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 3 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 3 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 4 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 4
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 4 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 5 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 5 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 6 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 6
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 6 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 7 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 7
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 7 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 8 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 8
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 8 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 9 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 9
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 9 }
			}
			add_corruption = 10
		}
		custom_tooltip = cabinet_access_variable_gain
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = stability_points 				which = corruption_stability_gain }
			# set_variable = { which = stability_points_to_go 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = prestige_available					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = greater_nobles_prestige_demand		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = prestige_needed					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = greater_nobles_prestige_trigger	value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = prestige_stability_gain			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = gift_ducat_cost					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = gift_stability_gain				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = corruption_cost					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = corruption_stability_gain			value = 0 }
			check_stability_gain = yes
			set_variable = { which = GN_favor_time_left					value = 60 }
		}
	}
	
	#option = { ### Grant Military Cabinet Position
	#	name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.003.e"
	#	ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	#}
	
	#option = {
	#	name = back
	#	highlight = yes
	#	
	#	trigger = {
	#		ai = no
	#		NOT = { has_dlc = "The Cossacks" }
	#	}
	#	
	#	country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Menu.020 }
	#}
	
	option = {
		name = exit
		highlight = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = one_estate_interaction
	}
}

country_event = { ### Demand Support
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.005
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.005.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.005.d"
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = eastern } picture = EE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = chinese } picture = EA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_GN_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	  which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a 		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a 		value = 5 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a		value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a		value = 1000 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					army_tradition = 0
				}
				set_variable = { which = army_leader_power 	value = 10 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						army_tradition = 10
					}
					change_variable = { which = army_leader_power  	value = 10 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							army_tradition = 20
						}
						change_variable = { which = army_leader_power  	value = 10 }
						if = {
							limit = {
								army_tradition = 30
							}
							change_variable = { which = army_leader_power  	value = 10 }
							if = {
								limit = {
									army_tradition = 40
								}
								change_variable = { which = army_leader_power  	value = 10 }
								if = {
									limit = {
										army_tradition = 50
									}
									change_variable = { which = army_leader_power  	value = 10 }
									if = {
										limit = {
											army_tradition = 60
										}
										change_variable = { which = army_leader_power  	value = 10 }
										if = {
											limit = {
												army_tradition = 70
											}
											change_variable = { which = army_leader_power  	value = 10 }
											if = {
												limit = {
													army_tradition = 80
												}
												change_variable = { which = army_leader_power  	value = 10 }
												if = {
													limit = {
														army_tradition = 90
													}
													change_variable = { which = army_leader_power  	value = 10 }
												}}}}}}}}}}
			#set_variable = { 	  which = army_leader_power_GN_added 						value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = army_leader_power_GN_added						which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = army_leader_power_GN_added 						value = 25 }
			change_variable = {   which = army_leader_power									which = army_leader_power_GN_added }
			
			#set_variable = {      which = estate_manpower							value = 0 }
			set_variable = {      which = estate_manpower							value = 100 }
			multiply_variable = { which = estate_manpower							which = estate_greater_nobles_treasury_annual }
			multiply_variable = {   which = estate_manpower							value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = estate_manpower							value = 1000 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Leader of Merit
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.005.a"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0

		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_loyalty		value = 0.11 }
			check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share	value = 0.10 }

	option = { ### Corvee
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.005.b"

			factor = 0

country_event = { ### Offensive War
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.007
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.007.t"
	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = GN_free_picks value = 1 } } }
		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.007.da"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = GN_free_picks value = 1 } }
		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.007.db"
	}
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = eastern } picture = EE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = chinese } picture = EA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_GN_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { ### Checking how many troops will be available for each option in the support event
			mil_tech_at_war_start = yes
			#set_variable = { 	  which = partial_infantry_support								value = 0 }
			#set_variable = { 	  which = partial_cavalry_support 								value = 0 }
			#set_variable = { 	  which = partial_artillery_support 							value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = partial_infantry_support								which = estate_greater_nobles_infantry }
			set_variable = { 	  which = partial_cavalry_support 								which = estate_greater_nobles_cavalry }
			set_variable = { 	  which = partial_artillery_support 							which = estate_greater_nobles_artillery }
			multiply_variable = {   which = partial_infantry_support								value = 0.25 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = partial_cavalry_support								value = 0.25 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = partial_artillery_support								value = 0.25 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = partial_infantry_support								value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = partial_infantry_support								value = 1000 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = partial_cavalry_support								value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = partial_cavalry_support								value = 1000 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = partial_artillery_support								value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = partial_artillery_support								value = 1000 }
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		ai = yes
			#	}
			#	set_variable = {	  which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a 						value = 0 }
			#}
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				set_variable = {	  which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a 						value = 5 }
			}
			#multiply_variable = {   which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a						value = 0.001 }
			#multiply_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a						value = 1000 }
			
			if = { ### Make sure you always get at least 1 infantry
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_infantry		value = 1 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = partial_infantry_support		value = 1 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = partial_infantry_support					value = 1 }
			}
			# partial_infantry_recruitment = yes
			# partial_cavalry_recruitment = yes
			# partial_artillery_recruitment = yes
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = full_infantry_support									value = 0 }
			#set_variable = { 	  which = full_cavalry_support 									value = 0 }
			#set_variable = { 	  which = full_artillery_support 								value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = full_infantry_support									which = estate_greater_nobles_infantry }
			set_variable = { 	  which = full_cavalry_support 									which = estate_greater_nobles_cavalry }
			set_variable = { 	  which = full_artillery_support 								which = estate_greater_nobles_artillery }
			#divide_variable = {   which = full_infantry_support								value = 1.3 }
			#divide_variable = {   which = full_cavalry_support									value = 1.3 }
			#divide_variable = {   which = full_artillery_support								value = 1.3 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = full_infantry_support								value = 0.5 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = full_cavalry_support								value = 0.5 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = full_artillery_support								value = 0.5 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = full_infantry_support									value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = full_infantry_support									value = 1000 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = full_cavalry_support									value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = full_cavalry_support									value = 1000 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = full_artillery_support								value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = full_artillery_support								value = 1000 }
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		ai = yes
			#	}
			#	set_variable = {	  which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_b 		value = 0 }
			#}
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				set_variable = { 	  which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_b 		value = 10 }
			}
			else = { set_variable = { 	  which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_b 	value = 5 } }
			#multiply_variable = {   which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_b		value = 0.001 }
			#multiply_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_b		value = 1000 }
			
			if = { ### Make sure you always get at least 1 infantry
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_infantry		value = 1 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = full_infantry_support		value = 1 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = full_infantry_support						value = 1 }
			}

country_event = { ### Demotion
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.008
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.008.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.008.d"
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = eastern } picture = EE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = chinese } picture = EA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_GN_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	  which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a 				value = 10 }
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a 				value = 20 }
			
			multiply_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a 				which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		is_variable_equal = {
			#			which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share
			#			value = 0
			#		}
			#	}
			#	
			#	# log = "<ERROR><93315500><THIS:[This.GetName]><PREV:[Prev.GetName]><ROOT:[Root.GetName]><FROM:[From.GetName]> Division by zero!"
			#	
			#}
			#else = {
				divide_variable = {
					which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a
					which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share
				}
			#}
			multiply_variable = {   which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a				value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a 				value = 1000 }
			
			if = { ### Insures the value gained does not exceed 100
				limit = {
					ai = yes
				}
				if = { ### Insures the value gained does not exceed 100
					limit = {
						check_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a		value = 30 }
					}
					set_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a			value = 30 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = { ### Insures the value gained does not exceed 100
					limit = {
						check_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a		value = 40 }
					}
					set_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a			value = 40 }
				}
			}
			#set_variable = { 	  which = milit_cost_a 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = milit_cost_a 			value = 300 }
			multiply_variable = { which = milit_cost_a 			which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = milit_cost_a 			value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = milit_cost_a 			value = 1000 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = stability_hit 		value = 50 }
			multiply_variable = { which = stability_hit 		which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share }
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Demote 20 percent with stability ###
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.008.a"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share 		value = 0.01 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a
		custom_tooltip = estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = promote_demote_nobles_time_left 		value = 120 }
			#set_variable = { 	which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed		which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a }
			estate_greater_nobles_loyalty_removed = yes
			#set_variable = { 	which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed		which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a }
			estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed = yes
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_global_flag = show_for_developers
			#	}
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_GN_demotion						value = 1 }
			#}
		}
		fight_corruption_stability = yes
		custom_tooltip = GN_demote_nobles
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight 	value = 0.001 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight			value = 0 }
			}
			set_variable = {	  which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_added		value = 0.20 }
			multiply_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_added		which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_country }
			change_variable = {   which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_added		value = 1 }
			change_variable = {   which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight			which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_added }
			
			#set_variable = {	  which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_check				value = 0 }
			set_variable = {	  which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_check				which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight }
			multiply_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_check				value = 5 }
			if = { ### Check to see if there are any greater Noble Promotions
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_check		which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_country }
				}
				# log = "BEGIN: POP_Estates_Interactions.008"
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = greater_nobles_control_province
					}
					#set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight			value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight			which = PREV }
				}
				while = {
					limit = {
						any_owned_province = {
							has_province_flag = greater_nobles_control_province
							NOT = { has_province_flag = time_to_demote }
							check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight	which = estate_weight }
						}
					}
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_flag = greater_nobles_control_province
							NOT = { has_province_flag = time_to_demote }
							check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight		which = estate_weight }
						}
						#set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract	value = 0 }
						set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract	which = estate_weight } ### set to weight in province
						
						#PREV = { set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract		value = 0 } }
						PREV = { set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract		which = PREV } }
						PREV = { subtract_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight			which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract } }
						#	set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract				value = 0 }
						set_province_flag = time_to_demote
					}
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_flag = greater_nobles_control_province
						}
						#set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight		value = 0 }
						set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight		which = PREV }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = POP_Estates.511
				}
				# log = "END: POP_Estates_Interactions.008"
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Demote 20 percent with military points ###
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.008.b"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 999
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = promote_demote_nobles_time_left 		value = 120 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a
		custom_tooltip = estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a
		custom_tooltip = milit_cost_a
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed		which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a }
			estate_greater_nobles_loyalty_removed = yes
			#set_variable = { 	which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed		which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a }
			estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed = yes
			#set_variable = { 	which = milit_cost 							value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = milit_cost							which = milit_cost_a }
			scaled_milit_cost_country = yes
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_global_flag = show_for_developers
			#	}
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_GN_demotion						value = 1 }
			#}
		}
		custom_tooltip = GN_demote_nobles
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight 	value = 0.001 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight			value = 0 }
			}
			set_variable = {	  which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_added		value = 0.20 }
			multiply_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_added		which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_country }
			change_variable = {   which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_added		value = 1 }
			change_variable = {   which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight			which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_added }
			#set_variable = {	  which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_check				value = 0 }
			set_variable = {	  which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_check				which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight }
			multiply_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_check				value = 5 }
			if = { ### Check to see if there are any greater Noble Promotions
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_check		which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_country }
				}
				# log = "BEGIN: POP_Estates_Interactions.008"
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = greater_nobles_control_province
					}
					#set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight			value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight			which = PREV }
				}
				while = {
					limit = {
						any_owned_province = {
							has_province_flag = greater_nobles_control_province
							NOT = { has_province_flag = time_to_demote }
							check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight 	which = estate_weight }
						}
					}
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_flag = greater_nobles_control_province
							NOT = { has_province_flag = time_to_demote }
							check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight		which = estate_weight }
						}
						#set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract		value = 0 }
						set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract		which = estate_weight } ### set to weight in province
						
						#PREV = { set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract		value = 0 } }
						PREV = { set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract		which = PREV } }
						PREV = { subtract_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight			which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract } }
						#	set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract				value = 0 }
						set_province_flag = time_to_demote
					}
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_flag = greater_nobles_control_province
						}
						#set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight			value = 0 }
						set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_promotion_weight 		which = PREV }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = POP_Estates.511
				}
				# log = "END: POP_Estates_Interactions.008"
			}
		}
	}

				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 1 }

					has_country_flag = LN_tax_exemptions_2_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = LN_tax_exemptions_3_flag
				}
				change_variable = { which = privilege_level value = 3 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {

				multiply_variable = {   which = LN_corruption_current			value = 0.01 }
				
				set_variable = {      which = LN_corruption_cost_1 			value = 0.1 }
				multiply_variable = { which = LN_corruption_cost_1			which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share }
			}
			#set_variable = { 	  which = privilege_stability_gain 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = privilege_stability_gain 				which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share }
			# change_variable = {   which = privilege_stability_gain				value = 0.15
			multiply_variable = { which = privilege_stability_gain 				value = 100 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = privilege_ticker_lesser_nobles value = 40 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = temp value = 40 }
				subtract_variable = { which = temp which = privilege_ticker_lesser_nobles }
				multiply_variable = { which = temp value = 0.025 }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { which = temp value = 0 }
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_a which = temp }
			multiply_variable = { which = privilege_stability_gain which = temp }
			check_stability_modifier = yes
		}
	}

	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.103.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.103.d"
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = eastern } picture = EE_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = chinese } picture = EA_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_LN_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	  which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_a 		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_a 		value = 5 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_a			value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_a			value = 1000 }
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_b 		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_b 		value = 5 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_b			value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_b			value = 1000 }
			
			check_stability_modifier = yes
			set_variable = {	  which = diplo_cost_a 							value = 30 } ### Diplomatic cost for gift
			multiply_variable = { which = diplo_cost_a 							which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = {   which = diplo_cost_a							value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = diplo_cost_a							value = 1000 }
			set_variable = {	  which = diplo_cost_b 							value = 90 } ### Diplomatic cost for gift
			multiply_variable = { which = diplo_cost_b 							which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = {   which = diplo_cost_b							value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = diplo_cost_b							value = 1000 }
			
			#set_variable = { which = prestige_available 	value = 0 }
			export_to_variable = {
				which = prestige_available
				value = prestige
			}
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand 	value = 0 }
			set_variable = {	  which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand 	which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand		value = 60 }
			set_variable = { which = prestige_needed 						which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand }
			divide_variable = {   which = prestige_needed					value = 10000 }
			multiply_variable = { which = prestige_needed					value = 10000 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = prestige_needed				value = 50 }
				}
				set_variable = { which = prestige_needed					value = 50 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = prestige_needed		value = 10 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = prestige_needed					value = 1 }
			}
			# set_variable = { 	  which = lesser_nobles_prestige_trigger 	value = 0 }
			# set_variable = { 	  which = lesser_nobles_prestige_trigger	which = prestige_available }
			# subtract_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_trigger	which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand }
			#set_variable = { 	  which = prestige_stability_gain 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = prestige_stability_gain			which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = prestige_stability_gain 			value = 20 }
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = ducat_cost_a 					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = ducat_cost_a 					which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_country }
			divide_variable = {   which = ducat_cost_a					value = 1.5 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = ducat_cost_a					value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = ducat_cost_a					value = 1000 }
			#set_variable = { 	  which = gift_stability_gain 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = gift_stability_gain			which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = gift_stability_gain 			value = 30 }

			#set_variable = { 	  which = corruption_cost 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = corruption_cost 				which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = corruption_cost				value = 10 }
			#set_variable = { 	  which = corruption_stability_gain 	value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = corruption_stability_gain		which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = corruption_stability_gain 	value = 20 }
			
			export_to_variable = { which = tmpTreasury value = treasury }
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Honor Prominent Nobleman
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.103.a"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10000
		}
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = prestige_available		which = prestige_needed }
			# check_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_trigger 	value = 0 }
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_a
		custom_tooltip = scaled_dip_cost_tooltip_a
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added				which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_a }
			estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_added = yes
			change_variable = { which = privilege_demand_ticker_lesser_nobles 	value = 2 }
			clr_country_flag = favor_LN_honor_nobleman_soon
			#change_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_action_ticker	value = 1 }
			#set_variable = { 	which = diplo_cost 							value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = diplo_cost							which = diplo_cost_a }
			scaled_diplo_cost_country = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand 			value = 0 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand 	value = 10 } }
			}
			add_prestige = -10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand 			value = 10 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand 	value = 20 } }
			}
			add_prestige = -20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand 			value = 20 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand 	value = 30 } }
			}
			add_prestige = -30
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand 			value = 30 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand 	value = 40 } }
			}
			add_prestige = -40
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand value = 50 }
			}
			add_prestige = -50
		}
		custom_tooltip = honor_noblemen_variable_gain
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = stability_points 				which = prestige_stability_gain }
			set_variable = { which = stability_points_to_go 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = prestige_available					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = prestige_needed					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_trigger		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = prestige_stability_gain			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = gift_ducat_cost					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = gift_stability_gain				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = corruption_cost					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = corruption_stability_gain			value = 0 }
			check_stability_gain = yes
			set_variable = { which = LN_favor_time_left					value = 60 }
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_global_flag = show_for_developers
			#	}
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_LN_favors_offered			value = 1 }
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_LN_honor_noble				value = 1 }
			#}
		}
	}
	option = { ### Offer Magnificent Gift
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.103.b"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

		}
		
		trigger = {
			#variable_arithmetic_trigger = {
			#	export_to_variable = {
			#		which = tmpTreasury
			#		value = treasury
			#	}
			#	
			#	check_variable = {
			#		which = tmpTreasury
			#		which = ducat_cost_a
			#	}
			#}
			check_variable = { which = tmpTreasury which = ducat_cost_a }
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_b
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added		which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_b }
			estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_added = yes
			clr_country_flag = favor_LN_present_gift_soon
		}
		custom_tooltip = scaled_dip_cost_tooltip_b
		custom_tooltip = ducat_cost_a
		custom_tooltip = magnificent_gift_variables_gain
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = {    which = ducat_cost 							value = 0 }
			set_variable = {    which = ducat_cost 							which = ducat_cost_a }
			change_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_treasury 		which = ducat_cost_a }
			#set_variable = { 	which = diplo_cost 							value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = diplo_cost							which = diplo_cost_b }
			scaled_diplo_cost_country = yes
			scaled_ducat_cost_country = yes
			change_variable = { which = stability_points 				which = gift_stability_gain }
			# set_variable = { which = stability_points_to_go 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = prestige_available					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = prestige_needed					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_trigger		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = prestige_stability_gain			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = gift_ducat_cost					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = gift_stability_gain				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = corruption_cost					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = corruption_stability_gain			value = 0 }
			check_stability_gain = yes
			set_variable = { which = LN_favor_time_left					value = 60 }
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_global_flag = show_for_developers
			#	}
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_LN_favors_offered			value = 1 }
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_LN_present_gift				value = 1 }
			#}
			set_variable = { which = tmpTreasury value = 0 }
		}
	}
	option = { ### Offer Low Level Special Cabinet Access
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.103.c"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ai = yes
					NOT = { corruption = 20 }
				}
				AND = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { corruption = 30 }
				}
			}
			#NOT = {
			#	corruption = 30
			#}
			#NOT = {
			#	AND = {
			#		ai = yes
			#		corruption = 10
			#	}
			#}
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_a
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added				which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_added_a }
			change_variable = { which = privilege_demand_ticker_lesser_nobles 	value = 2 }
			estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_added = yes
			clr_country_flag = favor_LN_corruption_soon
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 0 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 1 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 1 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 2 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 2 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 3 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 3 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 4 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 4
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 4 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 5 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 5 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 6 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 6
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 6 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 7 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 7
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 7 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 8 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 8
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 8 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 9 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 9
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 9 }
			}
			add_corruption = 10
		}
		
		#hidden_effect = {
		#	change_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_action_ticker	value = 1 }
		#}
		custom_tooltip = cabinet_access_variable_gain
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = stability_points 				which = corruption_stability_gain }
			# set_variable = { which = stability_points_to_go 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = prestige_available					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_demand		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = prestige_needed					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_prestige_trigger		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = prestige_stability_gain			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = gift_ducat_cost					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = gift_stability_gain				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = corruption_cost					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = corruption_stability_gain			value = 0 }
			check_stability_gain = yes
			set_variable = { which = LN_favor_time_left					value = 60 }
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_global_flag = show_for_developers
			#	}
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_LN_favors_offered			value = 1 }
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_LN_cabinet_posts			value = 1 }
			#}
		}
	}
	
	#option = { ### Grant Administrative Cabinet Position
	#	name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.103.e"
	#	ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	#}
	
	#option = {
	#	name = back
	#	highlight = yes
	#	
	#	trigger = {
	#		ai = no
	#		NOT = { has_dlc = "The Cossacks" }
	#	}
	#	
	#	country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Menu.100 }
	#}
	
	option = {
		name = exit
		highlight = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = one_estate_interaction
	}
}#

country_event = { ### Demand support
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.105
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.105.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.105.d"
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = eastern } picture = EE_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_LN_eventPicture }

country_event = { ### Promote Noble
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.107
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.107.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.107.d"
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = eastern } picture = EE_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = chinese } picture = EA_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_LN_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	  which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a 				value = 20 }
			multiply_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a 				which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share }
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		is_variable_equal = {
			#			which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share
			#			value = 0
			#		}
			#	}
			#	
			#	# log = "<ERROR><2AF302B0><THIS:[This.GetName]><PREV:[Prev.GetName]><ROOT:[Root.GetName]><FROM:[From.GetName]> Division by zero!"
			#	
			#}
			#else = {
				divide_variable = {
					which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a
					which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share
				}
			#}
			if = { ### Insures the value gained does not exceed 100
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a		value = 100 }
				}
				set_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a			value = 100 }
			}
			multiply_variable = {   which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a				value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a 				value = 1000 }
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = stability_gain_a 								value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = stability_gain_a 								which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = stability_gain_a 								value = 100 }
			
			check_stability_modifier = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Create Greater Nobility
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.107.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share 		value = 0.01 } }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = create_greater_nobility }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = create_greater_nobility
			set_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_treasury 		value = 100 }
			set_variable = { which = promote_demote_nobles_time_left 		value = 60 }
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_global_flag = show_for_developers
			#	}
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_LN_promote_nobles 				value = 1 }
			#}
		}
		add_adm_power = -50
		custom_tooltip = create_nobility
	}
	
	option = { ### Increase 20 percent
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.107.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share 		value = 0.01 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = promote_demote_nobles_time_left 		value = 120 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight 	value = 0.001 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight			value = 0 }
			}
			#set_variable = { 	  which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight_added			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight_added			value = 1 }
			multiply_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight_added			value = 0.2 }
			multiply_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight_added			which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_country }
			change_variable = {   which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight_added			value = 1 }
			change_variable = {   which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight					which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight_added }
			#set_variable = { 	  which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_check 					value = 0 }
			set_variable = {      which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_check					which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight }
			multiply_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_check					value = 5 }
			if = { ### Check to see if there are any Lesser Noble Promotions
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_check		which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_country }
				}
				# log = "BEGIN: POP_Estates_Interactions.107"
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = lesser_nobles_control_province
					}
					#set_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight		value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight 		which = PREV }
				}
				while = {
					limit = {
						any_owned_province = {
							has_province_flag = lesser_nobles_control_province
							NOT = { has_province_flag = time_to_promote }
							check_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight 	which = estate_weight }
						}
					}
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_flag = lesser_nobles_control_province
							NOT = { has_province_flag = time_to_promote }
							check_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight		which = estate_weight }
						}
						#set_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract 	value = 0 }
						set_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract		which = estate_weight } ### set to weight in province
						
						#PREV = { set_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract		value = 0 } }
						PREV = { set_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract		which = PREV } }
						PREV = { subtract_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight			which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract } }
						#	set_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight_subtract				value = 0 }
						set_province_flag = time_to_promote
					}
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_flag = lesser_nobles_control_province
						}
						#set_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight		value = 0 }
						set_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_promotion_weight 		which = PREV }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = POP_Estates.510
				}
				# log = "END: POP_Estates_Interactions.107"
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added		which = greater_nobles_loyalty_added_a }
			estate_greater_nobles_loyalty_added = yes
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_global_flag = show_for_developers
			#	}
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_LN_promote_nobles 				value = 1 }
			#}
		}
		custom_tooltip = stability_gain_a
		custom_tooltip = GN_promotion_may_not_fire
	}

		highlight = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	after = {

	}

				#set_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed		value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed 	which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_b }
				estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = LN_free_picks 	value = 1 }
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a
			custom_tooltip = recruitment_loyalty_cost_almost_free
			hidden_effect = {
				#set_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed		value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed 	which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a }
				estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed = yes
				subtract_variable = { which = LN_free_picks value = 1 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = LN_full_support
			if = { ### Used to determine how much extra forcelimit the player receives
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_logistical_support	value = 0.01 }	}
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_logistical_support			value = 0 }
			}
			change_variable = { which = estate_logistical_support			which = estate_logistical_support_full }
			
			#set_variable = { which = decided_infantry_support 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = decided_infantry_support 			which = full_infantry_support }
			#set_variable = { which = decided_cavalry_support 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = decided_cavalry_support 			which = full_cavalry_support }
			#set_variable = { which = decided_artillery_support 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = decided_artillery_support 			which = full_artillery_support }
			set_variable = { which = LN_infantry_fielded 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = LN_cavalry_fielded 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = LN_artillery_fielded 				value = 0 }
			# set_variable = { which = LN_infantry_fielded 				which = decided_infantry_support }
			# set_variable = { which = LN_cavalry_fielded 				which = decided_cavalry_support }
			# set_variable = { which = LN_artillery_fielded 				which = decided_artillery_support }
			
			set_country_flag = raised_special_units ### Is removed by POP_estate_levies.003, fired from on_actions at the end of a war
			set_country_flag = LN_offensive_war_help_full

				name = estate_war_support
				duration = 360
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = full_infantry_support 	value = 1 }
			}
			custom_tooltip = LN_infantry_full_gained
			hidden_effect = {
				estate_infantry_recruited = {
					estate_name = lesser_nobles
					estate_flag = lesser_nobles
					estate_prefix = LN
				}
				subtract_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_infantry	which = LN_infantry_fielded }
				set_variable = { which = LN_infantry_remaining					which = LN_infantry_fielded }
			}
		}
		if = {

	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_BUR_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = chinese } picture = EA_BUR_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_BUR_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_BUR_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_BUR_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = PrivilegeGrantingOngoing
			#set_variable = { 	  which = estate_weight_share 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = estate_weight_share 				which = estate_burghers_weight_share }
			set_variable = { 	  which = burghers_loyalty_added_a 			value = 20 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = burghers_loyalty_added_a			value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = burghers_loyalty_added_a			value = 1000 }
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				#set_variable = { 	  which = BG_corruption_current 		value = 0 }
				set_variable = {   which = BG_corruption_current 		which = privilege_corruption_BG }
				multiply_variable = {   which = BG_corruption_current			value = 0.01 }
				
				set_variable = {      which = BG_corruption_cost_1 			value = 0.1 }
				multiply_variable = { which = BG_corruption_cost_1			which = estate_burghers_weight_share }
			}
			#set_variable = { 	  which = privilege_stability_gain 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = privilege_stability_gain 				which = estate_burghers_weight_share }
			# change_variable = {   which = privilege_stability_gain				value = 0.15 }
			multiply_variable = { which = privilege_stability_gain 				value = 100 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = privilege_ticker_burghers value = 40 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = temp value = 40 }
				subtract_variable = { which = temp which = privilege_ticker_burghers }
				multiply_variable = { which = temp value = 0.025 }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { which = temp value = 0 }
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = burghers_loyalty_added_a which = temp }
			multiply_variable = { which = privilege_stability_gain which = temp }
			check_stability_modifier = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Tolerate Smuggling Rank 1
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.202.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 2000 }
		trigger = {
			has_global_modifier_value = {
				which = trade_efficiency
				value = 0.1
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = BG_tolerate_smuggling_1_flag }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = BG_tolerate_smuggling_2_flag }
		}
		BG_tolerate_smuggling_1 = yes
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_loyalty_added_a
		custom_tooltip = privilege_stability_gain
		BG_corruption_added_1_tooltip_effect = yes
		custom_tooltip = BG_tolerate_smuggling_1_privilege_desc
		
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	which = burghers_loyalty_added			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = burghers_loyalty_added			which = burghers_loyalty_added_a }
			estate_burghers_loyalty_added = yes
			change_variable = { which = stability_points 				which = privilege_stability_gain }
			set_variable = {    which = privilege_stability_gain 		value = 0  }
			set_variable = {    which = estate_weight_share 			value = 0  }
			set_variable = { 	which = BG_privileges_time_left			value = 60 }
			subtract_variable = { which = privilege_demand_ticker_burghers		value = 40 }
			check_stability_gain = yes
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_global_flag = show_for_developers
			#	}
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_BG_privileges_bestowed		value = 1 }
			#}
		}
	}
