country_event = { ### Offer Favors
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.203
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.203.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.203.d"
	picture = COURT_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	  which = burghers_loyalty_added_a 		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = burghers_loyalty_added_a 		value = 5 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = burghers_loyalty_added_a		value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = burghers_loyalty_added_a		value = 1000 }
			
			check_stability_modifier = yes
			set_variable = {	  which = diplo_cost_a 					value = 35 } ### Diplomatic cost for gift
			multiply_variable = { which = diplo_cost_a 					which = estate_burghers_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = {   which = diplo_cost_a					value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = diplo_cost_a					value = 1000 }
			#set_variable = { which = estate_weight_share 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = estate_weight_share 				which = estate_burghers_weight_share }

			#set_variable = {      which = autonomy_stability_gain 		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = autonomy_stability_gain		which = estate_burghers_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = autonomy_stability_gain 		value = 20 }

			#set_variable = { which = holiday_stability_gain 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = holiday_stability_gain				which = estate_burghers_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = holiday_stability_gain 		value = 15 }

			#set_variable = { 	  which = corruption_cost 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = corruption_cost 				which = estate_burghers_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = corruption_cost				value = 10 }
			#set_variable = { 	  which = corruption_stability_gain 	value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = corruption_stability_gain		which = estate_burghers_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = corruption_stability_gain 	value = 20 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Decade of self rule
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.203.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ai = yes
					NOT = { average_home_autonomy = 50 }
				}
				ai = no
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_loyalty_added_a
		custom_tooltip = scaled_dip_cost_tooltip_a
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	which = burghers_loyalty_added		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = burghers_loyalty_added		which = burghers_loyalty_added_a }
			estate_burghers_loyalty_added = yes
			#set_variable = { 	which = diplo_cost 					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = diplo_cost					which = diplo_cost_a }
			scaled_diplo_cost_country = yes
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_global_flag = show_for_developers
			#	}
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_BG_favors_offered		value = 1 }
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_BG_self_rule			value = 1 }
			#}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = stability_points 			which = autonomy_stability_gain }
			set_variable = { which = BG_favor_time_left				value = 60 }
			
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = burghers_control_province
				}
				add_local_autonomy = 25
			}
			check_stability_gain = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = autonomy_variable_gain
	}
	option = { ### Tax Holiday for Foreign Coin
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.203.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 1000 }
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ai = yes
					NOT = { inflation = 15 }
				}
				ai = no
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_loyalty_added_a
		custom_tooltip = scaled_dip_cost_tooltip_a
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = privilege_demand_ticker_burghers 	value = 2 }
			#set_variable = { 	which = burghers_loyalty_added				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = burghers_loyalty_added				which = burghers_loyalty_added_a }
			estate_burghers_loyalty_added = yes
			#set_variable = { 	which = diplo_cost 							value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = diplo_cost							which = diplo_cost_a }
			scaled_diplo_cost_country = yes
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_global_flag = show_for_developers
			#	}
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_BG_favors_offered		value = 1 }
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_BG_foreign_coin			value = 1 }
			#}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_weight_share 				value = 0.80 }
			}
			add_inflation = 4.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_weight_share 				value = 0.70 }
			}
			add_inflation = 4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_weight_share 				value = 0.60 }
			}
			add_inflation = 3.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_weight_share 				value = 0.50 }
			}
			add_inflation = 3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_weight_share 				value = 0.40 }
			}
			add_inflation = 2.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_weight_share 				value = 0.30 }
			}
			add_inflation = 2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_weight_share 				value = 0.20 }
			}
			add_inflation = 1.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_weight_share 				value = 0.10 }
			}
			add_inflation = 1
		}
		else = {
			add_inflation = 0.5
		}
		custom_tooltip = foreign_coin_variable_gain
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = stability_points 			which = holiday_stability_gain }
			set_variable = { which = BG_favor_time_left				value = 60 }
			check_stability_gain = yes
		}
	}
	option = { ### Offer Low Level Special Cabinet Access
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.203.c"
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ai = yes
					NOT = { corruption = 20 }
				}
				AND = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { corruption = 30 }
				}
			}
			#NOT = {
			#	AND = {
			#		ai = yes
			#		
			#		corruption = 10
			#	}
			#}
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_loyalty_added_a
		custom_tooltip = scaled_dip_cost_tooltip_a
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = privilege_demand_ticker_burghers 	value = 2 }
			#set_variable = { 	which = burghers_loyalty_added				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = burghers_loyalty_added				which = burghers_loyalty_added_a }
			estate_burghers_loyalty_added = yes
			#set_variable = { 	which = diplo_cost 							value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = diplo_cost							which = diplo_cost_a }
			scaled_diplo_cost_country = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 0 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 1 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 1 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 2 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 2 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 3 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 3 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 4 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 4
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 4 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 5 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 5 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 6 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 6
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 6 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 7 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 7
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 7 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 8 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 8
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 8 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 		value = 9 } }
			}
			add_corruption = 9
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = corruption_cost 				value = 9 }
			}
			add_corruption = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = stability_points 				which = corruption_stability_gain }
			#change_variable = { which = estate_burghers_action_ticker	value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = holiday_stability_gain				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = autonomy_stability_gain			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = diplo_cost_a						value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = gift_ducat_cost					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = gift_stability_gain				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = corruption_cost					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = corruption_stability_gain			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = BG_favor_time_left					value = 60 }
			check_stability_gain = yes
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_global_flag = show_for_developers
			#	}
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_BG_favors_offered			value = 1 }
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_BG_cabinet_posts			value = 1 }
			#}
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = cabinet_access_variable_gain
	}
	
	#option = { ### Grant Administrative Cabinet Position
	#	name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.203.e"
	#	ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	#}
	
	#option = {
	#	name = back
	#	highlight = yes
	#	
	#	trigger = {
	#		ai = no
	#		NOT = { has_dlc = "The Cossacks" }
	#	}
	#	
	#	country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Menu.030 }
	#}
	
	option = {
		name = exit
		highlight = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = one_estate_interaction
		set_variable = { which = autonomy_stability_gain value = 0 }
	}
}#

	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_BUR_eventPicture }

	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_BUR_eventPicture }

country_event = { ### Offensive War
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.207
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.207.t"
	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = BUR_free_picks 	value = 1 } } }
		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.207.da"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = BUR_free_picks 	value = 1 } }
		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.207.db"
	}
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_BUR_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_BUR_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = eastern } picture = EE_BUR_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_BUR_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = chinese } picture = EA_BUR_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_BUR_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_BUR_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_BUR_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		
		hidden_effect = { ### Burghers can contribute lots of money
			#set_variable = {	  which = burghers_loyalty_removed_a				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = burghers_loyalty_removed_a				value = 2 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = burghers_loyalty_removed_a				value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = burghers_loyalty_removed_a				value = 1000 }
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		ai = yes
			#	}
			#	set_variable = {	  which = burghers_loyalty_removed_b				value = 0 }
			#}
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				set_variable = { 	  which = burghers_loyalty_removed_b				value = 5 }
			}
			#multiply_variable = {   which = burghers_loyalty_removed_b				value = 0.001 }
			#multiply_variable = { which = burghers_loyalty_removed_b				value = 1000 }
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = estate_burghers_war_contribution 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = estate_burghers_war_contribution 			which = estate_burghers_treasury_annual }
			divide_variable = {   which = estate_burghers_war_contribution 			value = 1.5 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = estate_burghers_war_contribution			value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = estate_burghers_war_contribution			value = 1000 }
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = estate_burghers_logistical_support 		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = estate_burghers_logistical_support 		which = estate_burghers_treasury_annual }
			divide_variable = {   which = estate_burghers_logistical_support		value = 18 }
			multiply_variable = {   which = estate_burghers_logistical_support		value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = estate_burghers_logistical_support		value = 1000 }
			if = { ### Used to determine how much extra forcelimit the player receives
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_logistical_support	value = 1 }	}
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_logistical_support			value = 0 }
			}
			#set_variable = { 	  which = BUR_war_exhaustion_reduction 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = {      which = BUR_war_exhaustion_reduction			which = estate_burghers_treasury_annual }
			multiply_variable = { which = BUR_war_exhaustion_reduction 			value = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = country_total_pop value = 0 } }
				set_variable = { which = country_total_pop value = 1 } #MASKS AN ISSUE WITH DIVISION BY ZERO!!!
			}
			#else = {
				divide_variable = {
					which = BUR_war_exhaustion_reduction

country_event = { ### Assess Estate Loyalty
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.303
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.303.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.303.d"
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = eastern } picture = EE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = chinese } picture = EA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_GN_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	option = { # Effective Tax Rates
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.303.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		
		# Burghers
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_burghers_weight_share	value = 0.01 }
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_incomedisplay_BG
		}
		# Greater Nobles
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share	value = 0.01 }
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_incomedisplay_GN
		}
		# Lesser Nobles
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share	value = 0.01 }
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_incomedisplay_LN
		}
		
		country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Interactions.304 }
	}
	
	option = { # Influence Loyalty Shifts
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.303.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		custom_tooltip = estate_influencechange_display_desc
		# Burghers
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_burghers_weight_share	value = 0.01 }
			}
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = estate_burghers_influencechange_display	value = 1 } }
				custom_tooltip = estate_influencechange_display_BG_G
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_burghers_influencechange_display	value = -0.999 } } }
				custom_tooltip = estate_influencechange_display_BG_R
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = estate_influencechange_display_BG_Y
			}
		}
	
		# Greater Nobles
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share	value = 0.01 }
			}
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_influencechange_display	value = 1 } }
				custom_tooltip = estate_influencechange_display_GN_G
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_influencechange_display	value = -0.999 } } }
				custom_tooltip = estate_influencechange_display_GN_R
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = estate_influencechange_display_GN_Y
			}
		}
		
		# Lesser Nobles
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share	value = 0.01 }
			}
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_influencechange_display	value = 1 } }
				custom_tooltip = estate_influencechange_display_LN_G
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_influencechange_display	value = -0.999 } } }
				custom_tooltip = estate_influencechange_display_LN_R
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = estate_influencechange_display_LN_Y
			}
		}
		
		# Tribals
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_weight_share	value = 0.01 }
			}
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_influencechange_display	value = 1 } }
				custom_tooltip = estate_influencechange_display_TR_G
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_influencechange_display	value = -0.999 } } }
				custom_tooltip = estate_influencechange_display_TR_R
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = estate_influencechange_display_TR_Y
			}
		}
		
		country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Interactions.305 }
	}
	
	#option = {
	#	name = back
	#	highlight = yes
	#	
	#	ai_chance = {
	#		factor = 0
	#	}
	#	
	#	trigger = {
	#		ai = no
	#		NOT = { has_dlc = "The Cossacks" }
	#	}
	#	
	#	country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Menu.110 }
	#}
	
	option = {

		highlight = yes

			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

country_event = { ### Assess Estate Taxes
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.304
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.304.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.304.d"
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = eastern } picture = EE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = chinese } picture = EA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_GN_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#Loyalty
			set_variable = { which = EstateIncome_BG_Loyalty which = estate_burghers_loyalty }
			set_variable = { which = EstateIncome_GN_Loyalty which = estate_greater_nobles_loyalty }
			set_variable = { which = EstateIncome_LN_Loyalty which = estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty }
			#set_variable = { which = EstateIncome_FH_Loyalty which = estate_freeholders_loyalty }
			
			multiply_variable = { which = EstateIncome_BG_Loyalty value = 100 }
			multiply_variable = { which = EstateIncome_GN_Loyalty value = 100 }
			multiply_variable = { which = EstateIncome_LN_Loyalty value = 100 }
			#multiply_variable = { which = EstateIncome_FH_Loyalty value = 100 }
			
			#Loyalty Bonus
			set_variable = { which = EstateIncome_BG_LoyaltyMultiplier_percent which = EstateIncome_BG_LoyaltyMultiplier }
			set_variable = { which = EstateIncome_GN_LoyaltyMultiplier_percent which = EstateIncome_GN_LoyaltyMultiplier }
			set_variable = { which = EstateIncome_LN_LoyaltyMultiplier_percent which = EstateIncome_LN_LoyaltyMultiplier }
			#set_variable = { which = EstateIncome_FN_LoyaltyMultiplier_percent which = EstateIncome_FH_LoyaltyMultiplier }
			
			multiply_variable = { which = EstateIncome_BG_LoyaltyMultiplier_percent value = 100 }
			multiply_variable = { which = EstateIncome_GN_LoyaltyMultiplier_percent value = 100 }
			multiply_variable = { which = EstateIncome_LN_LoyaltyMultiplier_percent value = 100 }
			#multiply_variable = { which = EstateIncome_FH_LoyaltyMultiplier_percent value = 100 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = POP_Estates_Interactions.304.BG
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = estate_burghers_weight_share	value = 0.01 }
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = "estate_taxes_BG"
	}
	
	option = {
		name = POP_Estates_Interactions.304.GN
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_weight_share	value = 0.01 }
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = "estate_taxes_GN"
	}
	
	option = {
		name = POP_Estates_Interactions.304.LN
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_weight_share	value = 0.01 }
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = "estate_taxes_LN"
	}
	
	#option = {
	#	name = POP_Estates_Interactions.304.FH
	#	trigger = {
	#		check_variable = { which = estate_freeholders_weight_share	value = 0.01 }
	#	}
	#	
	#	custom_tooltip = "estate_taxes_FH"
	#}
	
	option = {
		name = back
		highlight = yes
		
		country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Interactions.303 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = exit
		highlight = yes

			factor = 100
		}
	}

### Category: Tribal Trust in Horde Leader

### Better military performance
### Higher tribute percentage
###




### Strategic Marriage (Unity, Loyalty, costs relation slot) (improves unity and loyalty each year, but not by much)
### Grant Authority to Tribal Leaders (improve loyalty, reduce unity)
### Plead for Order (stability point gain based on admin skill, must be under 0 stability, costs loyalty)
###	Gifts (small boost to unity and loyalty, cost to prestige, money, and glory)
### Demand Loyalty Oaths (improve unity, improve loyalty, costs glory)
### Crush rivals (stability loss chance, military based, gain decent unity and gain loyalty)

			estate_tribes_loyalty_added = yes

			#set_variable = { 	which = diplo_cost 									value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = diplo_cost									which = diplo_cost_a }
			scaled_diplo_cost_country = yes
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_global_flag = show_for_developers
			#	}
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_TR_authority						value = 1 }
			#	change_variable = { which = zzz_TR_favors 							value = 1 }
			#}
			set_variable = { which = TR_favor_time_left					value = 12 }
			set_country_flag = update_settlement_gravity
		}
		custom_tooltip = recent_advance_tribal_claims
	}
	
	
	#option = {
	#	name = back
	#	highlight = yes
	#	
	#	trigger = {
	#		ai = no
	#		NOT = { has_dlc = "The Cossacks" }
	#	}
	#	
	#	country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Menu.020 }
	#}
	
	option = {
		name = exit
		highlight = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = one_estate_interaction
		set_variable = { which = tribal_tribute_favor_display			value = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = update_settlement_gravity
			}
			clr_country_flag = update_settlement_gravity
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = tribals_ratio				value = 0.001 }
					is_city = yes
				}
				calc_settlement_score_gravity = yes # Recalculate the gravity
				tribals_settlement_calc = yes # Update tribal settlement score
				set_tribal_settlement = yes # Update modifiers
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { ### Renew tribal tribute
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.403
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.403.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.403.d"
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = chinese technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = western technology_group = eastern technology_group = indian technology_group = steppestech } } picture = MON_TRI_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = soudantech } } picture = ARAB_TRI_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech  } } picture = SEA_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american  } } picture = AMR_LN_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {	  which = admin_cost_a 							value = 50 }
			multiply_variable = { which = admin_cost_a 							which = estate_tribals_weight_share }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = ruler_admin_ability	value = 2 } }
				divide_variable = { which = admin_cost_a					which = ruler_admin_ability }
			}
			multiply_variable = {   which = admin_cost_a 							value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = admin_cost_a 							value = 1000 }
			
			
			### Grant Tribute ###
			set_variable = { which = tribes_loyalty_added_a						value = 0.334 }
			multiply_variable = { which = tribes_loyalty_added_a				which = ruler_diplo_ability }
			multiply_variable = {   which = tribes_loyalty_added_a 				value = 0.01 }
			multiply_variable = { which = tribes_loyalty_added_a 				value = 100 }
			### Grant Tribute ###
			#set_variable = { which = tribes_loyalty_removed_a 					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = tribes_loyalty_removed_a					value = 20 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = ruler_diplo_ability				value = 1 }
				}
				divide_variable = {   which = tribes_loyalty_removed_a 			which = ruler_diplo_ability }
			}
			multiply_variable = {   which = tribes_loyalty_removed_a 				value = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { which = tribes_loyalty_removed_a 				value = 1000 }
			
			set_variable = { which = tribal_tribute_favor_display			which = estate_tribals_treasury_annual }
			multiply_variable = { which = tribal_tribute_favor_display		value = 0.05 } # 5% of their income as tribute.
			multiply_variable = {   which = tribal_tribute_favor_display		value = 0.1 }
			multiply_variable = { which = tribal_tribute_favor_display		value = 10 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.403.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 75 }
		
		custom_tooltip = tribal_tribute_favor_cost
		tooltip = {
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = tribal_tribute_favor
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_tribes_loyalty_added_a_yearly
		add_prestige = -5
		custom_tooltip = scaled_adm_cost_tooltip_a
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	which = admin_cost 									value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = admin_cost									which = admin_cost_a }
			scaled_admin_cost_country = yes
			calc_tribal_tribute_favor = yes
			calc_misc_expenses = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = recent_tribal_tribute_use
	}

	option = {
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.403.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		
		remove_country_modifier = tribal_tribute_favor
		custom_tooltip = estate_tribes_loyalty_removed_a
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { 	which = tribes_loyalty_removed		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = tribes_loyalty_removed		which = tribes_loyalty_removed_a }
			estate_tribes_loyalty_removed = yes
			
			clr_country_flag = tribals_recieving_tribute
			set_variable = { which = tribal_tribute_favor				value = 0 }
			calc_misc_expenses = yes
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		set_variable = { which = tribal_tribute_favor_display			value = 0 }
	}
}

			check_variable = { which = education_state_contribute 	value = 100 }
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = education_state_contribute 				value = -100 }
			set_variable = { 	which = education_state_contribute_per_capita 	value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	which = education_church_contribute_per_capita 	value = 0 }
			calc_misc_expenses = yes
			country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Interactions.888 }
			set_variable = { which = education_target_L value = 0 }
		}
	}
	option = { ### Remove all funding
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.3022.h"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { 	  which = education_state_contribute 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = education_state_contribute_per_capita 	value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = education_church_contribute_per_capita 	value = 0 }
			calc_misc_expenses = yes
			country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Interactions.888 }
			set_variable = { which = education_target_L value = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {

		highlight = yes

		}

	}

country_event = { ### Plague Measures
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.307
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.307.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.307.d"
	picture = PLAGUE_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	option = { ### Discuss Closing Ports ###
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.307.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = plague_ports_closed }
			any_owned_province = {
				OR = {
					has_building = harbour_infrastructure_1
					has_building = harbour_infrastructure_2
					has_building = harbour_infrastructure_3x
					has_building = harbour_infrastructure_4
					has_building = harbour_infrastructure_5
				}
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Interactions.3071 }
		}
		if = { limit = { ai = yes }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = plague_measures_ai_pause
				duration = 15
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Discuss Restriction of Trade ###
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.307.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = trade_restricted }
			any_owned_province = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = minor_center_of_trade
					has_province_modifier = important_center_of_trade
					has_province_modifier = major_center_of_trade
					has_province_modifier = dominant_center_of_trade
				}
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Interactions.3072 }
		}
		if = { limit = { ai = yes }
			add_country_modifier = {

country_event = { ### Discuss Closing Ports
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.3071
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.3071.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.3071.d"
	picture = HARBOUR_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = country_port_percentage 		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = number_of_province 			value = 0 }
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_city = yes
				}
				#set_variable = { which = number_of_province 		value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = country_port_percentage	value = 0 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_port = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_building = harbour_infrastructure_1
						}
						change_variable = { which = country_port_percentage 	value = 1 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_building = harbour_infrastructure_2
						}
						change_variable = { which = country_port_percentage 	value = 2 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_building = harbour_infrastructure_3x
						}
						change_variable = { which = country_port_percentage 	value = 3 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_building = harbour_infrastructure_4
						}
						change_variable = { which = country_port_percentage 	value = 4 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_building = harbour_infrastructure_5
						}
						change_variable = { which = country_port_percentage 	value = 5 }
					}
					PREV = { change_variable = { which = country_port_percentage 	which = PREV } }
				}
				PREV = { change_variable = { which = number_of_province 		value = 1 } }
				#set_variable = { which = number_of_province 		value = 0 }
			}
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		is_variable_equal = {
			#			which = number_of_province
			#			value = 0
			#		}
			#	}

			#else = {
				divide_variable = {
					which = country_port_percentage
					which = number_of_province
				}
			#}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = ports_closing_checked }
				}
				#set_variable = {      which = diplo_cost_a 								value = 0 }
				set_variable = {      which = diplo_cost_a 								which = country_port_percentage }
				multiply_variable = { which = diplo_cost_a 								value = 50 }
				multiply_variable = {   which = diplo_cost_a								value = 0.001 }
				multiply_variable = { which = diplo_cost_a								value = 1000 }
				#set_variable = {      which = milit_cost_a 								value = 0 }
				set_variable = {      which = milit_cost_a 								which = country_port_percentage }
				multiply_variable = { which = milit_cost_a 								value = 25 }
				multiply_variable = {   which = milit_cost_a								value = 0.001 }
				multiply_variable = { which = milit_cost_a								value = 1000 }
				
				#set_variable = {      which = crisis_potential_b 						value = 0 }
				#set_variable = { 	  which = crisis_potential_b						which = country_port_percentage }
				#multiply_variable = { which = crisis_potential_b						value = 5 }
				#multiply_variable = { which = crisis_potential_b 						which = ports_burghers_resistance }
				
				#set_variable = {      which = burghers_loyalty_removed_a 				value = 0 }
				set_variable = { 	  which = burghers_loyalty_removed_a				which = ports_burghers_resistance }
				multiply_variable = { which = burghers_loyalty_removed_a				value = 5 }
				multiply_variable = {   which = burghers_loyalty_removed_a				value = 0.001 }
				multiply_variable = { which = burghers_loyalty_removed_a				value = 1000 }
			}

		}

country_event = { ### Assess Tribes
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.4011
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.4011.t"
	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_infantry_host value = 1 } } NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_cavalry_host value = 1 } } }
		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.4011.da"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_infantry_host value = 1 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_cavalry_host value = 1 } } }
		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.4011.db"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_infantry_host value = 1 } } check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_cavalry_host value = 1 } }
		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.4011.dc"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_infantry_host value = 1 } check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_cavalry_host value = 1 } }
		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.4011.dd"
	}
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = chinese technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = western technology_group = eastern technology_group = indian technology_group = steppestech } } picture = MON_TRI_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = soudantech } } picture = ARAB_TRI_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech  } } picture = SEA_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american  } } picture = AMR_LN_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_infantry_host	value = 1 } }
			}
			set_variable = { which = estate_tribals_infantry_host	value = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_cavalry_host	value = 1 } }
			}
			set_variable = { which = estate_tribals_cavalry_host	value = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = back
		highlight = yes
		
		trigger = {
			ai = no
		}
		
		country_event = { id = POP_Estates_Interactions.401 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = exit
		highlight = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}


country_event = { ### Raise Levies
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.407
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.407.t"
	desc = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_wealth value = 0.001 } }
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.407.d"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_wealth value = 0.001 } } }
		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.407.dalt"
	}
	#	desc = {
	#		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_wealth 	value = 1 } } NOT = { check_variable = { which = TR_free_picks 	value = 1 } } }
	#		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.407.da"
	#	}
	#	desc = {
	#		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_wealth 	value = 1 } } check_variable = { which = TR_free_picks 	value = 1 } }
	#		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.407.db"
	#	}
	#	desc = {
	#		trigger = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_wealth 	value = 1 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = TR_free_picks 	value = 1 } } }
	#		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.407.dc"
	#	}
	#	desc = {
	#		trigger = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_wealth 	value = 1 } check_variable = { which = TR_free_picks 	value = 1 } }
	#		desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.407.dd"
	#	}
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = chinese technology_group = turkishtech technology_group = western technology_group = eastern technology_group = indian technology_group = steppestech } } picture = MON_TRI_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = soudantech } } picture = ARAB_TRI_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech  } } picture = SEA_LN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american  } } picture = AMR_LN_eventPicture }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { ### Checking how many troops will be available for each option in the support event
			mil_tech_at_war_start = yes
			
			#ptm_subtribe_raise_all_precalc = yes
			
			set_variable = { 	  which = partial_infantry_support								value = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_infantry_loyal			value = 1 }
				}
				#set_variable = { 	  which = partial_infantry_support								value = 0 }
				set_variable = {   which = partial_infantry_support								which = estate_tribals_infantry_loyal }
				multiply_variable = {   which = partial_infantry_support								value = 0.25 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_tribal = no
					}
					set_variable = { 	  which = multiplier 								value = 0.7 }
					multiply_variable = { which = multiplier								which = estate_tribals_loyalty }
					change_variable = { which = multiplier									value = 0.3 }
					multiply_variable = { which = partial_infantry_support					which = multiplier }
					set_variable = { 	  which = multiplier 								value = 0 }
				}
				multiply_variable = {   which = partial_infantry_support								value = 0.001 }
				multiply_variable = { which = partial_infantry_support								value = 1000 }
			}
			
			set_variable = { 	  which = partial_cavalry_support 								value = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_cavalry_loyal			value = 1 }
				}
				#set_variable = { 	  which = partial_cavalry_support 								value = 0 }
				set_variable = {   which = partial_cavalry_support 								which = estate_tribals_cavalry_loyal }
				multiply_variable = {   which = partial_cavalry_support								value = 0.25 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_tribal = no
					}
					set_variable = { 	  which = multiplier 								value = 0.7 }
					multiply_variable = { which = multiplier								which = estate_tribals_loyalty }
					change_variable = { which = multiplier									value = 0.3 }
					multiply_variable = { which = partial_cavalry_support					which = multiplier }
					set_variable = { 	  which = multiplier 								value = 0 }
				}
				multiply_variable = {   which = partial_cavalry_support								value = 0.001 }
				multiply_variable = { which = partial_cavalry_support								value = 1000 }
			}
			
			if = { ### Make sure you always get at least 1 cavalry
				limit = {
					is_nomad = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_cavalry_loyal			value = 1 }
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = partial_cavalry_support		value = 1 } }
					}
					set_variable = { which = partial_cavalry_support						value = 1 }
				}
			}
			else_if = { ### Make sure you always get at least 1 infantry
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_infantry_loyal			value = 1 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = partial_infantry_support		value = 1 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = partial_infantry_support						value = 1 }
			}
			
			set_variable = { 	  which = full_infantry_support									value = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_infantry_loyal			value = 1 }
				}
				#set_variable = { 	  which = full_infantry_support									value = 0 }
				set_variable = {   which = full_infantry_support									which = estate_tribals_infantry_loyal }
				multiply_variable = {   which = full_infantry_support								value = 0.5 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_tribal = no
					}
					set_variable = { 	  which = multiplier 								value = 0.7 }
					multiply_variable = { which = multiplier								which = estate_tribals_loyalty }
					change_variable = { which = multiplier									value = 0.3 }
					multiply_variable = { which = full_infantry_support					which = multiplier }
					set_variable = { 	  which = multiplier 								value = 0 }
				}
				multiply_variable = {   which = full_infantry_support									value = 0.001 }
				multiply_variable = { which = full_infantry_support									value = 1000 }
			}
			
			set_variable = { 	  which = full_cavalry_support 									value = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_cavalry_loyal			value = 1 }
				}
				#set_variable = { 	  which = full_cavalry_support									value = 0 }
				set_variable = {   which = full_cavalry_support									which = estate_tribals_cavalry_loyal }
				multiply_variable = {   which = full_cavalry_support								value = 0.5 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_tribal = no
					}
					set_variable = { 	  which = multiplier 								value = 0.7 }
					multiply_variable = { which = multiplier								which = estate_tribals_loyalty }
					change_variable = { which = multiplier									value = 0.3 }
					multiply_variable = { which = full_cavalry_support					which = multiplier }
					set_variable = { 	  which = multiplier 								value = 0 }
				}
				multiply_variable = {   which = full_cavalry_support									value = 0.001 }
				multiply_variable = { which = full_cavalry_support									value = 1000 }
			}
			
			if = { ### Make sure you always get at least 1 cavalry
				limit = {
					is_nomad = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_cavalry_loyal			value = 1 }
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = full_cavalry_support		value = 1 } }
					}
					set_variable = { which = full_cavalry_support						value = 1 }
				}
			}
			else_if = { ### Make sure you always get at least 1 infantry
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_infantry_loyal			value = 1 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = full_infantry_support		value = 1 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = full_infantry_support						value = 1 }
			}
			
			#set_variable = {      which = estate_logistical_support_partial				value = 0 }
			set_variable = {   which = estate_logistical_support_partial				which = partial_infantry_support }
			change_variable = {   which = estate_logistical_support_partial				which = partial_cavalry_support }
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = estate_logistical_support_partial_display		value = 0 }
			set_variable = {   which = estate_logistical_support_partial_display		which = estate_logistical_support_partial }
			#change_variable = {   which = estate_logistical_support_partial_display		which = estate_logistical_support_partial_subtribe }
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = partial_raising_host_cost 					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = partial_raising_host_cost						which = estate_logistical_support_partial }
			multiply_variable = { which = partial_raising_host_cost						value = 15 }
						
			#set_variable = { 	  which = partial_raising_host_cost_display 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = {   which = partial_raising_host_cost_display 			which = partial_raising_host_cost }
			#change_variable = {   which = partial_raising_host_cost_display 			which = partial_raising_host_cost_subtribe }
			
			#set_variable = {      which = estate_logistical_support_full				value = 0 }
			set_variable = {   which = estate_logistical_support_full				which = full_infantry_support }
			change_variable = {   which = estate_logistical_support_full				which = full_cavalry_support }
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = estate_logistical_support_full_display		value = 0 }
			set_variable = {   which = estate_logistical_support_full_display		which = estate_logistical_support_full }
			#change_variable = {   which = estate_logistical_support_full_display		which = estate_logistical_support_full_subtribe }
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = full_raising_host_cost 						value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = full_raising_host_cost 						which = estate_logistical_support_full }
			multiply_variable = { which = full_raising_host_cost						value = 15 }
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = full_raising_host_cost_display				value = 0 }
			set_variable = {	  which = full_raising_host_cost_display				which = full_raising_host_cost }
			#change_variable = {	  which = full_raising_host_cost_display				which = full_raising_host_cost_subtribe }
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = partial_tribe_loot							value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = partial_tribe_loot							which = estate_tribals_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = partial_tribe_loot							value = 25 }
			
			#set_variable = { 	  which = full_tribe_loot								value = 0 }
			set_variable = { 	  which = full_tribe_loot								which = estate_tribals_weight_share }
			multiply_variable = { which = full_tribe_loot								value = 40 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Partial Support For War ###
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.407.a"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 10000
				has_country_flag = TR_war_part
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_loyalty		value = 0.11 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = TR_partial_support }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = TR_full_support }
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_flag = tribals_control_province
				NOT = { has_province_flag = was_occupied }
				is_overseas = no
				is_core = owner
			}
		}
		
		tribe_partial_loot_war_modifier = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = TR_partial_support
			#set_variable = { which = estate_tribals_wealth_at_war_start 	value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = estate_tribals_wealth_at_war_start 	which = estate_tribals_wealth }
			if = { ### Used to determine how much extra forcelimit the player receives
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_logistical_support	value = 0.01 }	}
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_logistical_support			value = 0 }
			}
			change_variable = { which = estate_logistical_support			which = estate_logistical_support_partial }
			
			#set_variable = {    which = decided_infantry_support 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = {    which = decided_infantry_support 			which = partial_infantry_support }
			#set_variable = {    which = decided_cavalry_support 			value = 0 }
			set_variable = {    which = decided_cavalry_support 			which = partial_cavalry_support }
			
			set_variable = {    which = TR_infantry_fielded 				value = 0 }
			set_variable = {    which = TR_cavalry_fielded 					value = 0 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_tribals_war_spent	value = 0.001 }	}
				}
				set_variable = { which = estate_tribals_war_spent			value = 0 }
			}
			change_variable = { which = estate_tribals_war_spent 			which = partial_raising_host_cost }
			subtract_variable = { which = estate_tribals_wealth				which = partial_raising_host_cost }
			
			set_country_flag = raised_special_units ### Is removed by POP_estate_levies.003, fired from on_actions at the end of a war
			set_country_flag = TR_offensive_war_help_partial
			
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = estate_war_support
				duration = 360
				hidden = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_nomad = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						mil = 5
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = tribal_maintenance_2
						duration = -1
						hidden = yes
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = tribal_maintenance_1
						duration = -1
						hidden = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_tribal = yes
					mil = 6
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = tribal_maintenance_0
					duration = -1
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { which = partial_infantry_support 	value = 1 }
					check_variable = { which = partial_cavalry_support 		value = 1 }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = TR_partial_gained
			hidden_effect = {
				estate_infantry_recruited = {
					estate_name = tribes
					estate_flag = tribals
					estate_prefix = TR
				}
				subtract_variable = { which = estate_tribals_infantry_loyal			which = TR_infantry_fielded }
				set_variable = { which = TR_infantry_remaining						which = TR_infantry_fielded }
				
				estate_cavalry_recruited = {
					estate_name = tribes
					estate_flag = tribals
					estate_prefix = TR
				}
				subtract_variable = { which = estate_tribals_cavalry_loyal		which = TR_cavalry_fielded }
				set_variable = { which = TR_cavalry_remaining					which = TR_cavalry_fielded }
			}
		}
		#if = {

				total_cavalry_share = TR_total_cavalry
			}
		}

		custom_tooltip = TR_logistical_support_partial
		custom_tooltip = tribe_mobilization_cost_partial
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { which = land_forcelimit						value = 0 }
			#set_variable = { which = army_size								value = 0 }

				which = land_forcelimit
				value = land_forcelimit
			}

				which = army_size
				value = army_size
			}
			#set_variable = { 	which = country_armed_forced_composite 		value = 0 } ### Mix of forcelimit and army size
			set_variable = { which = country_armed_forced_composite		which = land_forcelimit }
			multiply_variable = { which = country_armed_forced_composite		value = 0.5 } ### Scale it down
			change_variable = { which = country_armed_forced_composite		which = army_size }
			multiply_variable = { which = country_armed_forced_composite		value = 0.5 }
			change_variable = { which = country_armed_forced_composite		which = estate_logistical_support_partial }
			#set_variable = { 	which = estate_tribal_loot_share 			value = 0 } ### Used to determine how much loot the tribal estate will expect
			set_variable = { 	which = estate_tribal_loot_share 			which = estate_logistical_support_partial }

					which = estate_tribal_loot_share
					which = country_armed_forced_composite
				}
			#}
			set_variable = { which = country_armed_forced_composite value = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Full Support For Offensive War ###
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.407.c"

			factor = 1

			if = { ### Used to determine how much extra forcelimit the player receives

	after = {
			
		# Recalculate the total hosts
		#ptm_subtribe_add_all = yes

		#set_variable = { which = estate_tribals_cavalry_host			value = 0 }

		set_variable = { which = estate_tribals_total_soldiers 			which = estate_tribals_cavalry_host }
		change_variable = { which = estate_tribals_total_soldiers 			which = estate_tribals_infantry_host }
		
		set_variable = { which = full_infantry_support							value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = full_cavalry_support							value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = partial_infantry_support						value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = partial_cavalry_support						value = 0 }

		set_variable = { which = estate_logistical_support_partial_display		value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = partial_raising_host_cost 						value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = partial_raising_host_cost_display 				value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = estate_logistical_support_full					value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = estate_logistical_support_full_display			value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = full_raising_host_cost 						value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = full_raising_host_cost_display					value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = partial_tribe_loot								value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = full_tribe_loot								value = 0 }
		
		#set_variable = { which = ptm_partial_support_inf						value = 0 }
		#set_variable = { which = ptm_partial_support_cav						value = 0 }
		#set_variable = { which = ptm_full_support_inf							value = 0 }

		set_variable = { which = decided_cavalry_support 						value = 0 }
		
		clr_country_flag = one_estate_interaction
	}

country_event = { ### Collect special taxes event
	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.700
	title = "POP_Estates_Interactions.700.t"
	desc = "POP_Estates_Interactions.700.d"
	picture = HARBOUR_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = no
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a		value = 2 }
			#set_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a		value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a		value = 2 }
			set_variable = { which = ducat_gain								value = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = GN_special_taxes_ticker		value = 1 }
				}
				#set_variable = { 	  which = ducat_gain_a 				value = 0 }
				set_variable = { 	  which = ducat_gain_a 				which = estate_greater_nobles_treasury_annual }
				multiply_variable = {   which = ducat_gain_a				value = 0.5 }
				multiply_variable = {   which = ducat_gain_a				value = 0.001 }
				multiply_variable = { which = ducat_gain_a				value = 1000 }
				subtract_variable = { which = GN_special_taxes_ticker	value = 1 }
				change_variable = {   which = ducat_gain				which = ducat_gain_a }
				set_country_flag = GN_special_tax_applied
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = LN_special_taxes_ticker		value = 1 }
				}
				#set_variable = { 	  which = ducat_gain_b 				value = 0 }
				set_variable = { 	  which = ducat_gain_b 				which = estate_lesser_nobles_treasury_annual }
				multiply_variable = {   which = ducat_gain_b				value = 0.5 }
				multiply_variable = {   which = ducat_gain_b				value = 0.001 }
				multiply_variable = { which = ducat_gain_b				value = 1000 }
				subtract_variable = { which = LN_special_taxes_ticker	value = 1 }
				change_variable = {   which = ducat_gain				which = ducat_gain_b }
				set_country_flag = LN_special_tax_applied
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Collect Taxes ###
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.700.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GN_special_tax_applied
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a
			custom_tooltip = ducat_gain_a
			hidden_effect = {
				subtract_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_treasury		which = ducat_gain_a }
				#set_variable = { 	  which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed		value = 0 }
				set_variable = { 	  which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed		which = greater_nobles_loyalty_removed_a }
				estate_greater_nobles_loyalty_removed = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = LN_special_tax_applied
			}
			custom_tooltip = estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a
			custom_tooltip = ducat_gain_b
			hidden_effect = {
				subtract_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_treasury		which = ducat_gain_b }
				#set_variable = { 	  which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed		value = 0 }
				set_variable = { 	  which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed		which = lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed_a }
				estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty_removed = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scaled_ducat_gained_country = yes
			clr_country_flag = GN_special_tax_applied
			clr_country_flag = LN_special_tax_applied
			set_variable = { which = ducat_gain		value = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Rescind Taxes ###
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.700.b"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_greater_nobles_loyalty	value = 0.11 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = estate_lesser_nobles_loyalty		value = 0.11 } }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = GN_special_tax_applied
			clr_country_flag = LN_special_tax_applied
			set_variable = { which = GN_special_taxes_ticker 	value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = LN_special_taxes_ticker 	value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = ducat_gain					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = GN_special_taxes			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = LN_special_taxes			value = 0 }
		}
	}
}

	id = POP_Estates_Interactions.701

			set_variable = { which = LN_special_taxes_ticker 	value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = BUR_special_taxes_ticker 	value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = ducat_gain					value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = GN_special_taxes			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = LN_special_taxes			value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = BUR_special_taxes			value = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { ### Diplomatic option ###
		name = "POP_Estates_Interactions.701.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}
